           <ul acc-arrow-down="arrow-down" acc-arrow-up="arrow-up" class="abt_course" dir-accordion="">
            <li>
             <h4>
              What is this course about?
              <span class="acc-arrow">
              </span>
             </h4>
             <div class="pdp_faq">
              <p>
              </p>
              <div style="text-align: justify;">
               <strong>
                PMP
               </strong>
               training from Simplilearn is a unique, power packed, career-ready package and one of a kind in the industry. Participants enrolling for the training get the best of benefits as the course comprises of training in
               <strong>
                PMP
               </strong>
               , with
               <strong>
                free access
               </strong>
               to
               <strong>
                MS Project 2013 and PMI-ACP
               </strong>
               Online training courses.
               <br/>
               <br/>
               <strong>
                Project Management Professional (PMP) certification
               </strong>
               is the topmost professional certification for project managers offered by the Project Management Institute. Simplilearn, in response to the growing relevance of Agile methodology for Project Managers, is offering Agile Certified Practitioner (PMI-ACP) certification training along with PMP training, which equips Project Managers with the agile principles, practices, tools and techniques across agile methodologies.
              </div>
             </div>
            </li>
            <li>
             <h4>
              What learning benefits do you get from Simplilearns training?
              <span class="acc-arrow">
              </span>
             </h4>
             <div class="pdp_faq">
              <p>
              </p>
              <div style="text-align: justify;">
               Participants at the end of Simplilearns
               <strong>
                PMP training
               </strong>
               obtain the following learning benefits:
              </div>
              <ul>
               <li style="text-align: justify;">
                Understand the fundamentals of implementing standard processes and practices to be successful in their projects.
               </li>
               <li style="text-align: justify;">
                Enables professionals in providing effective project management delivery, which reduces costs, project duration and increase business value in organizations.
               </li>
               <li style="text-align: justify;">
                Establishes the participant's knowledge on all the five process groups and ten knowledge areas.
               </li>
              </ul>
              <div style="text-align: justify;">
               <strong>
                Benefits of MS Project
               </strong>
               <strong>
                training:
               </strong>
              </div>
              <ul>
               <li style="text-align: justify;">
                World's Most popular Project Management Tool
               </li>
               <li style="text-align: justify;">
                Develops documenting and vital project management skills
               </li>
               <li style="text-align: justify;">
                Enhanced skills for creating, executing, consolidating and splitting projects.
               </li>
               <li style="text-align: justify;">

               </li>

              <div style="text-align: justify;">
               <strong>
                Benefits of
               </strong>
               <strong>
                PMI-ACP training:
               </strong>
              </div>
              <ul>
               <li style="text-align: justify;">
                Demonstrate expertise in agile principles, practices, tools and techniques
               </li>
               <li style="text-align: justify;">
                Increase professional versatility in project management tools and techniques
               </li>

               </li>

               </li>
              </ul>
             </div>
            </li>
            <li>
             <h4>
              What are the career benefits in-store for you?
              <span class="acc-arrow">
              </span>
             </h4>
             <div class="pdp_faq">
              <p>
              </p>
              <div style="text-align: justify;">
               A Certified PMP professional will have an upward career graph.
              </div>
              <ul>
               <li style="text-align: justify;">
                According to brighthubpm.com, one of leading websites for project management in the world, PMP certified project managers receive an average starting salary of $92,000 (Indeed.com) a year. Overall the PMP credentials will gain you a 20 percent increase in salary over non-credentialed project managers with similar qualifications.
               </li>
               <li style="text-align: justify;">
                The process of becoming PMP certified enlarges the individuals professional network and helps in their career path.
               </li>
               <li style="text-align: justify;">
                An individual with a PMP certification along with complete knowledge of MS project are most sought-after by Fortune 500 companies globally.
               </li>
               <li style="text-align: justify;">

        <div class="exam-and-certification-wrapper">
         <h3>
          Exam &amp; Certification
         </h3>
         <div class="exam-certification">
          <div class="exam-certi-section">
           <div class="course-faq">
            <ul acc-arrow-down="arrow-down" acc-arrow-up="arrow-up" dir-accordion="">
             <li>
              <div>
               <h4>
                How do you become PMP certified professional?
                <span class="acc-arrow">
                </span>
               </h4>
              </div>
              <div class="pdp_faq">
               <p>
               </p>
               <div style="text-align: justify;">
                <span style="line-height: 20.7999992370605px;">
                 First, you should become a PMI member before applying for the PMP examination. Becoming a member is a fairly straightforward process and can be completed online at www.pmi.org. Make sure you enter the contact details and name correctly. This is important so that you don't miss any information sent to you later. Also, ensure that the details on the certification are correct.
                </span>
                <br style="line-height: 20.7999992370605px;"/>
                <br style="line-height: 20.7999992370605px;"/>
                <span style="line-height: 20.7999992370605px;">
                 The duration of PMP exam is four hours. It covers 200 questions, out of which 25 are considered as pre-test questions and are included by PMI to see how many test takers get them right. Based on this, they might decide to include these questions in a future exam. It is similar to a survey conducted by PMI. Of the 200 questions, therefore, 175 will be scored. All questions are multiple-choice questions, with only one correct answer.
                </span>
                <br style="line-height: 20.7999992370605px;"/>
                <br style="line-height: 20.7999992370605px;"/>
                <span style="line-height: 20.7999992370605px;">
                 You get one point for every question answered correctly. There is no negative marking for the incorrect ones. You may also mark a question that you are unsure of and revisit it at the end. However, you should attempt all 200 questions in the given time.
                </span>
                <br style="line-height: 20.7999992370605px;"/>
                <br style="line-height: 20.7999992370605px;"/>
                <span style="line-height: 20.7999992370605px;">
                 PMI grades students on each of the five process groups, and based on the grading, they declare a test taker as PMP pass or fail. The grades are not disclosed to everyone. Rather, a rating is given in each of the five process groups. The rating can be Below Proficient, Proficient, and Moderately Proficient
                </span>
                <br style="line-height: 20.7999992370605px;"/>
                <br style="line-height: 20.7999992370605px;"/>
                <span style="line-height: 20.7999992370605px;">
                 The result (pass or fail) is determined by a combination of these grades. The number of grades or points one has to score to pass the PMP exam is not made public by PMI.
                </span>
               </div>
              </div>
             </li>
             <li>
              <div>
               <h4>
                What are the prerequisites for the certification?
                <span class="acc-arrow">
                </span>
               </h4>
              </div>
              <div class="pdp_faq">
               <p>
                To apply for the PMP exam, candidates need to have:
               </p>
               <table border="1" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0">
                <tbody>
                 <tr>
                  <td style="width: 213px; text-align: center;">
                   <strong>
                    Educational Background
                   </strong>
                  </td>
                  <td style="width:213px;">
                   <strong>
                    Project Management Experience
                   </strong>
                  </td>
                  <td style="width:213px;">
                   <strong>
                    Project Management Education
                   </strong>
                  </td>
                 </tr>
                 <tr>
                  <td style="width: 213px; text-align: center;">
                   Secondary degree ? High school Diploma, Associates degree or global equivalent
                  </td>
                  <td style="width: 213px; text-align: center;">
                   Minimum 5 Years/60 months unique non-overlapping professional project management experience during which at least 7500 hours are spent leading and directing project tasks*
                  </td>
                  <td style="width: 213px; text-align: center;">
                   35 contact hours of formal project management education
                  </td>
                 </tr>
                 <tr>
                  <td colspan="3" style="width: 638px; text-align: center;">
                   <strong>
                    Or
                   </strong>
                  </td>
                 </tr>
                 <tr>
                  <td style="width: 213px; text-align: center;">
                   Bachelors degree or global equivalent
                  </td>
                  <td style="width: 213px; text-align: center;">
                   Minimum 3 years/36 months unique non-overlapping professional project management experience during which at least 4500 hours are spent in leading and directing project tasks*
                  </td>
                  <td style="width: 213px; text-align: center;">
                   35 contact hours of formal project management education
                  </td>
                 </tr>
                 <tr>
                  <td colspan="3" style="width: 638px; text-align: center;">
                   *Leading and directing project tasks as identified in the PMP Exam Specification. Within the total hours of project management experience, experience in all five process groups of project management is required. However, on a single project, you do not need to have experience in all five process groups.
                  </td>
                 </tr>
                </tbody>
               </table>
              </div>
             </li>
             <li>

                <span class="acc-arrow">

               </h4>

             </li>
            </ul>

             <h4>
              Who provides the certification?
              <span class="acc-arrow">

             </h4>
             <div class="pdp_faq">
              <p>
               We provide training for attaining the PMP certification from the reputed PMI Institute.
              </p>
             </div>
            </li>
            <li ng-style="{display:(fsc.isCurrentFaqType('Online Self Learning')) ? 'block' : 'none'}">
             <h4>
              How do I track the hours already spent on the course?
              <span class="acc-arrow">
              </span>
             </h4>
             <div class="pdp_faq">
              <p>
               You can track the number of hours spent on the course by accessing your LMS home.
              </p>

              </span>
             </h4>
             <div class="pdp_faq">
              <p>
               Yes, we offer course completion certificate after you successfully complete the training program.
              </p>
             </div>
            </li>
            <li ng-style="{display:(fsc.isCurrentFaqType('Online Self Learning')) ? 'block' : 'none'}">
             <h4>
              Do you provide contact hours after completing the training? How many hours of PDU certificate do I get after attending the training?
              <span class="acc-arrow">
              </span>
             </h4>
             <div class="pdp_faq">
              <p>
               Yes, we offer PDU certificate to candidates after successfully completing the training. You can earn 35 contact hours certificate after attending the training.
              </p>
             </div>

            <li ng-style="{display:(fsc.isCurrentFaqType('Online Self Learning')) ? 'block' : 'none'}">
             <h4>
              Do you provide any group discounts for online training programs?
              <span class="acc-arrow">
              </span>
             </h4>
             <div class="pdp_faq">
              <p>
               Yes, we have group discount packages for online training programs. Contact support@simplilearn.com to know more about the group discounts.
              </p>
             </div>
            </li>
            <li ng-style="{display:(fsc.isCurrentFaqType('Online Self Learning')) ? 'block' : 'none'}">
             <h4>
              Why should I choose PMI Certification and not any other project management certification? What makes PMIs special?
              <span class="acc-arrow">
              </span>
             </h4>
             <div class="pdp_faq">
              <p>
              </p>
              <ol>
               <li>
                PMI certifications are not based on one specific methodology, so theyre flexible and adaptable. You can easily transfer them between industries, market segments and geographic locations.
               </li>
               <li>
                PMI continually conducts in-depth studies to ensure that our credentials reflect the current skills, knowledge and best practices needed to succeed.
               </li>
               <li>
                You will never have to worry about a PMI certification becoming obsolete. Our certification maintenance program requires you to earn a professional development unit (PDUs), which encourages you to continually develop your skills and stay up to date as the profession changes.
               </li>
               <li>
                PMI certification offers financial benefits  the Project Management Professional (PMP)  credential increases your salary by up to 10%, according to the PMI Salary Survey  Sixth Edition, 2009and helps you stand out and better market yourself to prospective employers.
               </li>
               <li>
                PMI has provided project management certifications for over 25 years, and our PMP credential was the first one designed specifically for project managers.
               </li>
              </ol>
             </div>
            </li>
            <li ng-style="{display:(fsc.isCurrentFaqType('Online Self Learning')) ? 'block' : 'none'}">
             <h4>
              Which certification exams does PMI offer?
              <span class="acc-arrow">
              </span>
             </h4>
             <div class="pdp_faq">
              <p>
               PMI offers five different exams related to the discipline of Project Management. These are:
              </p>
              <ol>
               <li>
                PgMP: Program Management Professional
               </li>
               <li>
                PMP: Project Management Professional
               </li>
               <li>
                CAPM: Certified Associate in Project Manager
               </li>
               <li>
                PMI-SP: PMI Scheduling Professional
               </li>
               <li>
                PMI-RMP: PMI Risk Management Professional
               </li>
               <li>
                PMI-ACP: PMI Agile Certified Practitioner
               </li>
              </ol>
             </div>
            </li>
            <li ng-style="{display:(fsc.isCurrentFaqType('Online Self Learning')) ? 'block' : 'none'}">
             <h4>
              How many questions are there in the PMP certification exam?
              <span class="acc-arrow">
              </span>
             </h4>
             <div class="pdp_faq">
              <p>
               It covers 200 questions, out of which 25 questions are considered as pre-test questions used for future tests and are not scored. You will not be communicated about these questions; they are randomly chosen. Therefore, you should answer all 200 questions with the same seriousness.
              </p>
             </div>
            </li>
            <li ng-style="{display:(fsc.isCurrentFaqType('Online Self Learning')) ? 'block' : 'none'}">
             <h4>
              What is the duration of the PMP exam?
              <span class="acc-arrow">
              </span>
             </h4>
             <div class="pdp_faq">
              <p>
               The PMP exam is conducted for four hours.
              </p>
             </div>
            </li>
            <li ng-style="{display:(fsc.isCurrentFaqType('Online Self Learning')) ? 'block' : 'none'}">
             <h4>
              Are there any pointers provided by Simplilearn for the exam?
              <span class="acc-arrow">
              </span>
             </h4>
             <div class="pdp_faq">
              <p>
               Yes. Simplilearn provides exam tips and brain dumps which are specially designed keeping the certification exam in mind. These tips work as a ready reckoner and help the candidates to clear the exam in first attempt.
              </p>
             </div>
            </li>
            <li ng-style="{display:(fsc.isCurrentFaqType('Online Self Learning')) ? 'block' : 'none'}">
             <h4>
              How does Simplilearn assure that the material and the training delivered are effective?
              <span class="acc-arrow">
              </span>
             </h4>
             <div class="pdp_faq">
              <p>
              </p>
              <div style="text-align: justify;">
               All our courses are aligned with globally approved UAPA framework (Understand, Apply, Practice and Access) which incorporates a four-phased course development process and helps the candidates to clear the exam in first attempt.
              </div>
             </div>
            </li>
            <li ng-style="{display:(fsc.isCurrentFaqType('Online Self Learning')) ? 'block' : 'none'}">
             <h4>
              Will I get the PMP certificate after completing this PMP certification course?
              <span class="acc-arrow">
              </span>
             </h4>
             <div class="pdp_faq">
              <p>
               On completing the PMP certification course from Simplilearn, you will get a course-completion certificate from Simplilearn. PMP certification can be obtained by appearing for the PMI Certified PMP exam. The number of grades or points that one has to score to pass the PMP exam is not made public by PMI.
              </p>
             </div>
            </li>
            <li ng-style="{display:(fsc.isCurrentFaqType('Online Self Learning')) ? 'block' : 'none'}">
             <h4>
              Is exam fee included in the course fee?
              <span class="acc-arrow">
              </span>
             </h4>
             <div class="pdp_faq">
              <p>
               Exam fee is not included in the course fee and the user will have to pay an exam fee to appear for PMP certification exam.
              </p>

         Terms &amp; Conditions
        </strong>

       <div class="pop_in_bl">
        <div class="money_bk_in">
         <p>
          4-day PMP Boot Camp with 100% Money back guarantee
         </p>
         <p>
          <span class="text_line">
           Standard Terms &amp; Conditions
          </span>
         </p>
         <ul>
          <li>
           In 4-day PMP Boot Camp with 100% money back, the re-examination fee is paid by us and the remaining amount is refunded, if you do not clear PMP exam.
          </li>
          <li>
           To ensure 100% success or money back, the PMP exam is to be taken within 30 days of the completion of the classroom training.
          </li>
          <li>
           If the exam is not cleared in the first attempt, we provide reimbursement for the re-examination fees.
          </li>
          <li>
           Participants need to take the re-exam within 30 days from the result date of the 1st attempt.
          </li>
          <li>
           If the exam is not cleared in the 2nd attempt, we provide reimbursement for your PMP re-examination fees.
          </li>
          <li>
           Participants need to take the re-exam within 30 days from the result date of the 2nd attempt.
          </li>
          <li>
           If the exam is not cleared in the 3rd attempt (maximum number of attempts permissible by PMI in a year), we provide refund of the balance of enrollment fees paid by you at the time of enrollment.
          </li>
          <li>
           PMP participants need to provide their PMP exam scoreboards in order to get the reimbursement for course fee.
          </li>
          <li>
           PMP participants are required to pay the PMP re-examination fees directly to the PMI. We will be reimbursing the fees subsequently.
          </li>
         </ul>
         <br/>
         <table>
          <tr>
           <th>
            Attempt
           </th>
           <th>
            Time frame
           </th>
           <th>
            Result
           </th>
           <th>
            Money back
           </th>
          </tr>
          <tr>
           <td>
            1st
           </td>
           <td>
            1-month from course completion
           </td>
           <td>
            Not Cleared
           </td>
           <td>
            $275 Re-Exam Fees
           </td>
          </tr>
          <tr>
           <td>
            2nd
           </td>
           <td>
            1-month from the 1st attempt
           </td>
           <td>
            Not Cleared
           </td>
           <td>
            $275 Re-Exam Fees
           </td>
          </tr>
          <tr>
           <td>
            3rd
           </td>
           <td>
            1-month from the 2nd attempt
           </td>
           <td>
            Not Cleared
           </td>
           <td>
            Refund balance of enrollment fees
           </td>
          </tr>
         </table>
         <br/>
         <p>
          <span class="text_line">
           Money Back Guarantee: Reimbursement Process
          </span>
         </p>
         <ul>
          <li>
           PMP participants are required to send scanned copies of their PMP scorecards of each attempt to support@simplilearn.comalong with the PMP Boot Camp location and date.
          </li>
          <li>
           We will reimburse the amount payable within 30 days of receiving all the documents.
          </li>
          <li>
           The mode of reimbursement will be same as the mode of payment used during enrollment fees. For example: If a PMP participant has paid through PayPal, we will reimburse through PayPal only.
          </li>
          <li>
           Money back guarantee is applicable only for Simplilearn's 4-day PMP Boot Camp and not for online PMP training and 2-day PMPSpeedPrep courses
          </li>
         </ul>
         <br/>
         <p>
          <span class="text_line">
           When Money Back Guarantee is void?
          </span>
         </p>
         <ul>
          <li>
           Participants did not take the PMP examination within 30 days of the classroom training completion date.
          </li>
          <li>
           Participants not taking the re-exam within 30 days of the previous attempt result date.
          </li>
          <li>
           Participants not maintaining 100% attendance in the 4-day PMPBoot Camp.
          </li>
          <li>
           Participants not going through the e-learning content. 8 hours of online study is required for to familiarize with the PMP course.
          </li>
          <li>
           Failing to score at least 80% in any 3 of the 5 available online PMP simulation tests at Simplilearn.com.
          </li>
          <li>
           Participants not following the instructions and completing the exercises given in the 4-day PMP Boot Camp.
          </li>
          <li>
           Participants not submitting the required documents to Simplilearn.
          </li>
         </ul>

document.onkeydown = function (event) {
	
	if (!event) { /* This will happen in IE */
		event = window.event;
	}
		
	var keyCode = event.keyCode;
	
	if (keyCode == 8 &amp;&amp;
		((event.target || event.srcElement).tagName != "TEXTAREA") &amp;&amp; 
		((event.target || event.srcElement).tagName != "INPUT")) { 
		
		if (navigator.userAgent.toLowerCase().indexOf("msie") == -1) {
			event.stopPropagation();
		} else {
			
			event.returnValue = false;
		}
		
		return false;
	}
};
